<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">у-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">u-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-стила́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-stilátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:устилать.html>устила́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">ustilátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:устлать.html>устла́ть</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">устели́ть</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to cover the whole surface of; to carpet, to pave, etc.</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:устойчивый.html>усто́йчивый</a> (6091)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:устоять.html>устоя́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">ustojátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-чивый</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-čivyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:устойчивый.html>усто́йчивый</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">ustójčivyj</span>) (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)усто́йчивее</b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)усто́йчивей</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>steady, stable
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:устойчивый.html>усто́йчивое</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:положение.html>положе́ние</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>ustójčivoje</b> položénije</i> ― <span class="e-translation">stable position</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:устойчивый.html>усто́йчивое</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:словосочетание.html>словосочета́ние</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>ustójčivoje</b> slovosočetánije</i> ― <span class="e-translation">idiom</span> (literally, “<span class="e-literally">stable phrase</span>”)</div></dd></dl></li>
<li>steadfast, resistant to external influence
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:устойчивый.html>усто́йчивое</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:убеждение.html>убежде́ние</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>ustójčivoje</b> ubeždénije</i> ― <span class="e-translation">steadfast belief</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>hardy, resistant <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">of plants or animals</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></li>
<li>sustainable
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:устойчивый.html>усто́йчивое</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:развитие.html>разви́тие</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>ustójčivoje</b> razvítije</i> ― <span class="e-translation">sustainable development</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

***устоять.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:устоять.html>устоя́ть</a> (7613)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">у-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">u-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:стоять.html>стоя́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">stojátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:устоять.html>устоя́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">ustojátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">уста́ивать</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to keep one's balance, to remain on one's feet, to stand one's ground, to stand fast
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:устоять.html>устоя́ть</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">ne <b>ustojátʹ</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">to lose (one's) ground</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to resist, to withstand, to stand up <i>(against)</i>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:устоять.html>устоя́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:перед.html>пе́ред</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:искушение.html>искуше́нием</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>ustojátʹ</b> péred iskušénijem</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to resist the temptation</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li>The imperfective form <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">уста́ивать</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">ustáivatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> is uncommon.</li></ul>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Derived_terms">Derived terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:устояться.html>устоя́ться</a> (16149)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:устоять.html>устоя́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">ustojátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:устраивать.html>устра́ивать</a> (2068)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:устроить.html>устро́ить</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">ustróitʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ивать</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ivatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:устраивать.html>устра́ивать</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">ustráivatʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:устроить.html>устро́ить</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to arrange, to organize, to establish
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:устраивать.html>устра́ивать</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:демонстрация.html>демонстра́ции</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>ustráivatʹ</b> demonstrácii</i> ― <span class="e-translation"><b>to organize</b> demonstrations</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to make
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:устраивать.html>устра́ивать</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:скандал.html>сканда́л</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>ustráivatʹ</b> skandál</i> ― <span class="e-translation"><b>to make</b> a scandal</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to settle, to put in order</li>
<li>to place, to fix up, to set up</li>
<li>to suit, to satisfy, to be convenient</li></ol>

***устраиваться.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:устраиваться.html>устра́иваться</a> (6172)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:устраивать.html>устра́ивать</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">ustráivatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:устраиваться.html>устра́иваться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">ustráivatʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:устроиться.html>устро́иться</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to settle down, to get settled
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:устраиваться.html>устра́иваться</a></b> поудо́бнее</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>ustráivatʹsja</b> poudóbneje</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to make oneself comfortable</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:устраиваться.html>устра́иваться</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:работа.html>рабо́ту</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>ustráivatʹsja</b> na rabótu</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to get fixed up in a job, to get a job, to apply for a job</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to turn out right, to get fine, to be OK
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>Не</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:беспокоиться.html>беспоко́йся</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:мама.html>ма́ма</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:весь.html>всё</a> <b>устра́иватся</b>.</i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Ne bespokójsja, máma, vsjó <b>ustráivatsja</b>.</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">Don't worry, mum, everything will be OK (will come out alright).</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">passive of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:устраивать.html>устра́ивать</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">ustráivatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>

***устраняться.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:устраняться.html>устраня́ться</a> (28423)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:устранять.html>устраня́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">ustranjátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:устраняться.html>устраня́ться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">ustranjátʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">устрани́ться</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to disappear, to be eliminated</li>
<li>to stop participating, to pull away <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:от.html>от́</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">ot</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + genitive, from something</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></li>
<li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">passive of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:устранять.html>устраня́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">ustranjátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>

***устрашение.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:устрашение.html>устраше́ние</a> (26519)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">устраши́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">ustrašítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-е́ние</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-énije</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:устрашение.html>устраше́ние</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">ustrašénije</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:устрашение.html>устраше́ния</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:устрашение.html>устраше́ния</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:устрашение.html>устраше́ний</a></b>)

<li>frightening</li>
<li>deterrence</li></ol>

***устремить.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:устремить.html>устреми́ть</a> (8151)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">у-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">u-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">стреми́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">stremítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:устремить.html>устреми́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">ustremítʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:устремлять.html>устремля́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to rush</li>
<li>to turn <i>(to)</i>, to direct <i>(at, towards)</i>, to fix <i>(on, upon)</i>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:устремить.html>устреми́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:взор.html>взор</a> (<a href = vnd.unilang:к.html>к</a>)</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>ustremítʹ</b> vzor (k)</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to turn one's eyes (to, towards)</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:устремить.html>устреми́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">ustremítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
